 Like the State Bank, there are five other public sector banks whose NPA has increased so much that the Reserve Bank of India has warned them to do something immediately
 sarkari report bataati he ki aam bhartiya kaa 63 fisadi paisa saarvajaniki kshetra ke bainkon main jamaa he, 18 fisadi hi nijee bainkon main jamaa he
 If these public sector banks submerge, a large number of customers will be affected
 mira nangiya ne likhaa he ki bel-in naam se ek praavdhaan aa rahaa he jo prastaavit rejolushan corporation ko adhikaar degaa ki vah bainkon kii libility ko radd kar de yani yaa bank lambey samay tak ke liye nivesh kar de, aapako de hi na
 The money you deposit in banks with a fixed deposit or common deposit is called liability
 bank aapse vaada karata he ki aap jab paisa maangenge tab vah lautaa degaa
 Now after the arrival of this Bell Inn, it is being said that banks can refuse to give you money
 ho saktaa he ki badale main aapako kuch share de den, koi security de den
 Our colleague Sushil Mahapatra has spoken to Meera Nangia
 dilli uniwarsity kii cormas kii associat professor mira nangiya ne bataaya ki FRDI Bill agar paas hua to Resolution Corporation tay karegaa ki har customer apni jamaa puunji ke kitne hissaa kaa beemaa kara sakegaa
 We may have a different percentage in the same bank, there may be a different percentage for you
 banking vishyon par hindi main likhane vaale vibhaash kumaar shrivastav se bhi hamane is masale par or samajhane kaa prayaas kiya
 It is certain that after the introduction of these provisions, the relationship between the customer and the bank will change
 kai jaankaron ne likhaa he ki bainkon main ab aapkaa paisa surakshit nahin rahegaa
 Either the money will sink or the bank will invest that money somewhere for its own sake
 jis tarah se aap kisi company kaa share kharidte hai usee tarah se bainkon main paisa jamaa karnaa ho jayega
 This is a big change
 banking association ke logon ne kaha he ki vah bhi is bill ke praavdhaan se sahamat nahin hai
 The Congress, Trinamool Congress and CPM have called the bill anti-people
 28 november ko congress ne press release jari kiya he
 The Congress has said that the health of most public sector banks is poor
 iskaa matlab yah hua ki in bainkon main jamaa aapkaa paisa surakshit nahin he
 If this bill is passed then the weaker sections of the society will be deeply shocked, their money deposited in banks will be drowned
 aam aadmi party ke pravaktaa raghav chaddha ne 7 disambar ko press conferes kar yahi ashanka zaahir kii he
 The bail-out is now going to be a bail-in for the bank
 matlab, pehle jab koi bada udyogpati kisi bank ko lone waapas nahin karata tha or bank kangaali kii kagaar par aa jaataa tha to sarkaar apni jeb se paise dekar us bank kii madad karti thi jise bel-out package bhi kehete hai
 But now through this law, a bail-in system will be made, that is, the bank will grab the money of the common people of the country which is deposited in their bank accounts and will compensate the industrialists by forgiving the loan
 or ye sabakuch aapaki marzi ke bina kiya jayega
 The comments is kram main cyprus main hue ek prayog kaa bhi udhaaharan diya ja rahaa he
 But such an experiment was not successful there
 is kanoon ke aane ke baad vahaan ke aam logon kaa paisa bainkon ne hadap liya
 After these criticisms, the government has said that the government is committed to protecting the customer's money
 vitt mantri arun jetali ne twit kiya he ki finantial rezeulation and deposit insurance bill sansad kii sthaayee samiti ke adheen he
 The government's intention is to protect the interests of financial institutions and account holders
 yahi nahin vitt mantralay kii taraf se ek safai bhi ai he
 In which it is said that misconceptions are being spread in the media about the provisions of the bail-in bill
 sansad main jo bill pesh kiya gaya he usase khataadharakon kii maujuuda suraksha main koi badlaav nahin kiya gaya he
 The bill includes new provisions for account holders in a transparent manner
 dekhte hai sansadeey samiti is maamle main kya report detii he
 - After demonetisation, the government is now eyeing your bank account, bringing a new bill - kya jaanate hai aap, bank main rakhaa paisa hi nahin rahegaa aapkaa, lut sakati he sari jamaa puunji - Your money kept in the bank will not be yours, Modi government is bringing new law kya vaaki aisa hone ja rahaa he, bill main to he magar antim rup se hoga, abhi nahin kaha ja saktaa, magar jo he us par baat ho sakati he
 On 9 November, Meera Nangia wrote a detailed article on this in The Hindu newspaper, then there was a doubt in the mind of many that whether it is really possible that banks can refuse to return our money
 iske baad 3 disambar ko scrol par shruti sagar ne is par likhaa or phir dhire-dhire kai jagahon par yah khabar chhapane lagi
 The new provisions say that the money deposited by the account holders can be used to bail out the bank
 diposit insurance and credit guarantee korporation bhi khatm kiya janaa he
 Under which the account holders have been guaranteed to return up to Rs 1 lakh
 abhi tak kanoon he ki aapke khate main agar das lakh jamaa he, bank dub gaya to sirf ek lakh tak milegaa
 Consider nine lakh rupees as drowned
 isaki jagah bainkon ko chhot di jaaegi ki wo aapkaa paisa lautaaenge yaa nahin
 If returned, in what form
 kahin lambey samay ke liye nivesh kar diya to aap gaye kaam se
 npas of banks have increased from 6 lakh crores
 bainkon ke liye yah buree khabar to hoti hi he, aapke liye bhi he kyonki bank doobenge to aapkaa paisa bhi dubegaa
 According to the new provision, drowning banks will be asked to save themselves, do not give money to the account holder
 vivaad bill ke chapter 4 section 2 ko lekar bhi he
 According to this, after consulting the resolution corporation regulator, it will decide that the Financial Resolution and Deposit Insurance Bill
 diwalia bank ke jamakarta ko uske jamaa paise ke badale kitni rakam di jaae

 9 november ko da hindu akhbaar main mira nangiya ne is par vistaar se lekh likhaa to kai logon ke man main yah ashanka uthi ki kya vaaki aisa ho saktaa he ki bank hamaare paise ko lautaane se inkaar kar sakate hai
 After this, on December 3, Shruti Sagar wrote on the scroll and then slowly this news began to be published in many places
 nae praavdhaanon main kaha gaya he ki khataadharakon ke jamaa paise kaa istemaal bank ko ubaarane main kiya ja saktaa he
 Deposit Insurance and Credit Guarantee Corporation is also to be scrapped
 jiske tahat khataadharakon ko 1 lakh rupee tak lautaani kii guarantee mili he
 As of now, there is a law that if there is a million deposited in your account, if the bank is drowned then you will get only one lakh
 nau lakh rupaya samajhie dub gaya
 Instead banks will be given a discount on whether they will return your money or not
 agar lautaaenge to kis rup main
 If you invested for a long time, you went to work
 bainkon kaa enpie badhkar 6 lakh karod se bad gaya he
 This is bad news for the banks, it is also for you because if the banks sink, your money will also drown
 nae praavdhaan ke anusaar duubate bainkon se kaha jayega ki aap khud hi bachaa lo, khatadharak ko paisa mat do
 The dispute is also related to Chapter 4 section 2 of the bill
 iske mutabik rezolution corporation regaulator se salaah-mashvire ke baad ye tay karegaa ki finantial rezeulation and deposit insurance bill
 How much money should be given to the bankrupt bank's depositor in exchange for his deposited money
 wo tay karegaa ki jamakarta ko koi khaas rakam mili yaa phir khate main jamaa puraa paisa
 State Bank's non-performing asset NPA increased to Rs 1,88,069 crore in June 2017
 state bank kii tarah hi paanch anya sarkari bank hai jinka enpie itnaa bad gaya he ki bhartiya reserve bank ne unhen tatkaal kuch karne kii chetavanee di he
 Government reports show that 63 per cent of the money of the common Indian is deposited in public sector banks, only 18 per cent is in private banks
 agar ye saarvajanik kshetra ke bank duube to badi sankhya main customer prabhavit ho jaaenge
 Meera Nangia has written that a provision is coming in the name of Bell-in which will empower the proposed resolution corporation to cancel the liability of the banks i
e
, or the bank invests for a long time, you should not
 jo paisa aap bainkon main fiks deposit yaa aam deposit jamaa karte hai use libility kehete hai
 The bank promises you to return the money when you ask for it
 ab is bel in ke aane ke baad kaha ja rahaa he ki bank aapako paisa dene se manaa kar sakate hai
 Maybe give you some shares in return, give some security
 hamaare sahyogi susheel mahapatra ne mira nangiya se baat kii he
 Meera Nangia, Associate Professor, Cormus, Delhi University, said that if the FRDI bill is passed, the Resolution Corporation will decide how much of its accumulated capital will be insured by each customer
 ek hi bank main hamaare liye alag pratisht ho saktaa he aapke liye alag pratisht ho saktaa he
 We also tried to understand more on this issue from Vibhash Kumar Srivastava, who wrote in Hindi on banking subjects
 yah to tay he ki bel in praavdhaan ke aane ke baad customer or bank ke bich kaa rishta badal jayega
 Many experts have written that your money will no longer be safe in banks
 yaa to paisa dub jayega yaa phir us paise ko bank apni khatir kahin nivesh kar degaa
 The way you buy shares of a company, it will be like depositing money in banks
 yah ek bada badlaav he
 People of the banking association have said that they too do not agree with the provision of this bill
 congress, trinmul congress or sipiem ne is bill ko janvirohi kaha he
 On 28 November, Congress has issued a press release
 congress ne kaha he ki zyaadaatar saarvajanik kshetron ke bainkon kii sehat karaab he
 This means that your money deposited in these banks is not safe
 agar yah bill paas ho gaya to samaaj ke kamazor tabake ko gaharaa dhakka pahonchega, bainkon main jamaa unka paisa dub jayega
 Aam Aadmi Party spokesperson Raghav Chadha has expressed this apprehension by press conference on 7 December
 bank ke liye ab bail- out darasal bail-in banane ja rahaa he
 Meaning, earlier when a big industrialist did not return a loan to a bank and the bank was on the verge of bankruptcy, the government used to help the bank which is also known as bail-out package by giving money from its pocket
 lekin ab is kanoon ke zarie bel-in system bana diya jayega yani desh ke aam logon kaa paisa jo unke bank khaaton main jamaa he, use bank hadap legaa or udyogpatiyon kaa lone maaf karte hue apane nuksaan kii bharpai kar legaa
 And all this will be done without your consent
 tippaniyan An example is also being given of an experiment done in Cyprus in this order
 magar vahaan aisa prayog safal nahin rahaa tha
 After the introduction of this law, the money of the common people of the people was grabbed by the banks
 in aalochanaon ke baad sarkaar ne kaha he ki sarkaar customer ke paise kii suraksha ko lekar patibaddh he
 Finance Minister Arun Jaitley tweeted that the Financial Resolutions and Deposit Insurance Bill is under the standing committee of Parliament
 sarkaar kii manshaa vittiya sansthaanon or khataadharakon ke hiton ko surakshit rakhana he
 Not only this, a clarification has also come from the Finance Ministry
 jisamen kaha gaya he ki media main bill main bel-in ke praavdhaanon ko lekar galatfahami failaai ja rahi he

 bill main pardarshi tareeke se khataadharakon ke liye suraksha ke nae praavdhaan shaamil kiye gaye hai
